## STR (Red) (191)

### Tier 1

#### Amanamu's Tithe
- **Tags**: Support, Lineage, Minion, Persistent
- **Category**: Amanamu's Tithe
- **Requires**: Level 25
- **Description**: Supports Persistent Minion Skills, granting a chance when Supported Minions die for you to gain an Abyssal Monster Modifier.
- **Mods**: 50% chance to gain an Abyssal Monster Modifier for 20 seconds when a Minion from Supported Skills dies / Maximum 3 Abyssal Monster Modifiers gained this way
- **Supported Skills** (22): Skeletal Warrior, Skeletal Reaver, Skeletal Brute, Skeletal Sniper, Skeletal Frost Mage, Skeletal Storm Mage, Skeletal Arsonist, Skeletal Cleric, Wolf Pack, Rhoa Mount, Raging Spirits, Grim Feast, Summon Infernal Hound, Navira, the Last Mirage, Ruzhan, the Blazing Sword, Kelari, the Tainted Sands, Kelari's Malediction, Sacrifice, Ravenous Swarm, Companion: {0}, Manifest Weapon, Supporting Fire

#### Armour Demolisher I
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Armour Demolisher
- **Description**: Supports any skill, causing Armour Break it inflicts to be stronger.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills Break 50% more Armour

#### Armour Explosion
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, Warcry, AoE, Trigger, Fire, Payoff
- **Category**: Armour Explosion
- **Description**: Supports Attacks and Warcries, causing them to trigger a Fiery explosion when they Fully Break an enemy's Armour.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills trigger an Explosion when they Fully Break an enemy's Armour
- **Supported Skills** (133): Leap Slam, Shield Charge, Flicker Strike, Armour Breaker, Rain of Arrows, Falling Thunder, Lightning Arrow, Herald of Ice, Herald of Thunder, Infernal Cry, Rolling Magma, Earthquake, Sunder, Seismic Cry, Earthshatter, Boneshatter, Volcanic Fissure, Rapid Assault, Disengage, Blood Hunt, Whirling Slash, Spearfield, Lightning Spear, Glacial Lance, Whirling Assault, #### Atalui's Bloodletting
- **Tags**: Support, Lineage, Physical
- **Category**: Lifetap
- **Requires**: Level 65
- **Description**: Supports any Skill, turning a portion of its Mana cost into a Life cost. Does not support Skills which reserve Spirit. Supported Skills Gain a portion of their Life cost as extra Physical Damage.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have Mana Costs Converted to Life Costs

#### Auto Reload
- **Tags**: Support, Ammunition, Projectile
- **Category**: Auto Reload
- **Description**: Supports Crossbow Ammunition Skills, causing them to automatically reload when they Heavy Stun an enemy.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills reload automatically when Heavy Stunning an enemy with them
- **Supported Skills** (16): High Velocity Rounds, Fragmentation Rounds, Siege Cascade, Armour Piercing Rounds, Explosive Shot, Incendiary Shot, Rapid Shot, Glacial Bolt, Permafrost Bolts, Hailstorm Rounds, Ice Shards, Plasma Blast, Galvanic Shards, Stormblast Bolts, Shockburst Rounds, Crossbow Shot

#### Battershout
- **Tags**: Support, Warcry, AoE, Trigger, Physical, Payoff
- **Category**: Battershout
- **Description**: Supports Warcry Skills. Supported Skills Consume Fully Broken Armour to trigger Physical Damage explosions on Enemies within their range but cannot themselves Break Armour.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills cannot Break Armour
- **Supported Skills** (6): Infernal Cry, Seismic Cry, Fortifying Cry, Lunar Blessing, Arctic Howl, Ancestral Cry

#### Bloodlust
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, Melee, Physical
- **Category**: Bloodlust
- **Description**: Supports Melee Attacks, causing them to deal more damage against Bleeding enemies, but preventing them from inflicting Bleeding.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills deal 30% more Melee Physical Damage against Bleeding enemies
- **Supported Skills** (63): Leap Slam, Shield Charge, Flicker Strike, Armour Breaker, Falling Thunder, Earthquake, Sunder, Earthshatter, Boneshatter, Volcanic Fissure, Rapid Assault, Disengage, Blood Hunt, Whirling Slash, Spearfield, Whirling Assault, Rolling Slam, Supercharged Slam, Wind Blast, Wave of Frost, Ice Strike, Glacial Cascade, Killing Palm, Shattering Palm, Rampage, Furious Slam, Tempest Flurry, Staggering Palm, Siphoning Strike, Tempest Bell, Frozen Locus, Perfect Strike, Raise Shield, Resonating Shield, Thunderous Leap, Hammer of the Gods, Stampede, Shield Wall, Punch, Quarterstaff Strike, Flail Strike, Sword Slash, Axe Slash, Mace Strike, Claw Stab, Dagger Stab, Spear Stab, Vaulting Impact, Storm Wave, Gathering Storm, Primal Strikes, Cull The Weak, Fangs of Frost, Wind Serpent's Fury, Rake, Parry, Elemental Sundering, Wing Blast, Fury of the Mountain, Cross Slash, Lunar Assault, Devour, Forge Hammer

#### Brutus' Brain
- **Tags**: Support, Lineage, Minion
- **Category**: Meat Shield
- **Requires**: Level 65
- **Description**: Supports skills which create Minions, causing those Minions to be unable to deal or take Damage. Cannot support skills which create undamageable Minions.
- **Mods**: Minions from Supported Skills cannot be Damaged
- **Supported Skills** (26): Raise Zombie, Bone Offering, Skeletal Warrior, Skeletal Reaver, Skeletal Brute, Skeletal Sniper, Skeletal Frost Mage, Skeletal Storm Mage, Skeletal Arsonist, Skeletal Cleric, Wolf Pack, Pain Offering, Unearth, Rhoa Mount, Raging Spirits, Soul Offering, Summon Infernal Hound, Navira, the Last Mirage, Ruzhan, the Blazing Sword, Kelari, the Tainted Sands, Kelari's Malediction, Ancestral Spirits, Ravenous Swarm, Companion: {0}, Manifest Weapon, Supporting Fire

#### Cirel's Cultivation
- **Tags**: Support, Lineage, Totem
- **Category**: Totemic Control
- **Requires**: Level 65
- **Description**: Supports Skills which create Totems, preventing you from having more than one of that Totem but granting significant benefits for Supported Totems based how many allied Totems are near them. Does not Support Skills used by Minions.
- **Mods**: Totems created by Supported Skills have 5% increased area of effect per allied Totem in effect radius
- **Supported Skills** (4): Shockwave Totem, Siege Ballista, Artillery Ballista, Dark Effigy

#### Compressed Duration I

- **Mods**: Supported Skills have 30% less Skill Effect Duration

#### Daresso's Passion
- **Tags**: Support, Banner, Lineage
- **Category**: Daresso's Passion
- **Requires**: Level 65
- **Description**: Supports Banner Skills, causing them to require significantly less Glory to use.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills require 50% less Glory to use
- **Supported Skills** (3): War Banner, Defiance Banner, Dread Banner

#### Dauntless
- **Tags**: Support, Conditional
- **Category**: Dauntless
- **Description**: Supports Skills you use yourself which can cause Damaging Hits. Supported Skills cannot be used unless you have been stationary for a certain duration, but deal increasingly more damage the longer you are stationary. Cannot support Skills which have a reservation, are Triggered, have a cooldown or have another usage Condition.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills cannot be used unless you have been stationary for 1.5 seconds / This timer resets when you move
- **Supported Skills** (146): Firebolt, Ice Nova, Leap Slam, Shield Charge, Detonate Dead, Volatile Dead, Flicker Strike, Spark, Enervating Nova, Lightning Warp, Armour Breaker, Rain of Arrows, #### Double Barrel I
- **Tags**: Support, Ammunition, Projectile
- **Category**: Double Barrel
- **Description**: Supports Crossbow Ammunition Skills, causing them to load an extra bolt at the cost of reload speed.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have 30% less Reload Speed
- **Supported Skills** (16): High Velocity Rounds, Fragmentation Rounds, Siege Cascade, Armour Piercing Rounds, Explosive Shot, Incendiary Shot, Rapid Shot, Glacial Bolt, Permafrost Bolts, Hailstorm Rounds, Ice Shards, Plasma Blast, Galvanic Shards, Stormblast Bolts, Shockburst Rounds, Crossbow Shot

#### Efficiency I
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Efficiency
- **Description**: Supports any skill, making it cost less to use. Cannot support skills which reserve Spirit.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have 30% less Cost

#### Einhar's Beastrite
- **Tags**: Support, Lineage, Attack, Melee, Strike
- **Category**: Behead
- **Requires**: Level 65
- **Description**: Supports Melee Strike skills, causing them to steal a Modifier from Rare monsters they kill for a lengthy duration, while being unable to damage enemies not on low Life. Does not modify skills used by Minions.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills can only Damage Low Life Enemies
- **Supported Skills** (29): Flicker Strike, Armour Breaker, Boneshatter, Rapid Assault, Disengage, Blood Hunt, Whirling Slash, Whirling Assault, Ice Strike, Killing Palm, Shattering Palm, Tempest Flurry, Staggering Palm, Siphoning Strike, Perfect Strike, Punch, Quarterstaff Strike, Flail Strike, Sword Slash, Axe Slash, Mace Strike, Claw Stab, Dagger Stab, Spear Stab, Primal Strikes, Cull The Weak, Fangs of Frost, Rake, Lunar Assault

- **Tags**: Support, Fire
- **Category**: Eternal Flame

#### Tireless

- **Category**: Tireless

#### Uhtred's Augury
- **Tags**: Support, Lineage
- **Category**: Uhtred of Kalguur
- **Requires**: Level 65
- **Description**: Supports Skills which can gain levels, granting them many additional levels provided exactly two other supports are used with the supported Skill. Does not support skills which do not have levels.
- **Mods**: +3 to level of Supported Skills if exactly two other Supports are modifying them

#### Uhtred's Exodus
- **Tags**: Support, Lineage
- **Category**: Uhtred of Kalguur
- **Requires**: Level 65
- **Description**: Supports Skills which can gain levels, granting them many additional levels provided no other supports are used with the supported Skill. Does not support skills which do not have levels.
- **Mods**: +3 to level of Supported Skills if no other Supports are modifying them

### Tier 3

#### Armour Break II
- **Tags**: Support, Physical
- **Category**: Armour Break
- **Description**: Supports Skills that Hit Enemies, causing those Hits to Break Armour based on a portion of Physical Damage dealt. On Fully Breaking Armour with Supported Skills, you have a chance to gain an Endurance Charge.
- **Mods**: Break Armour equal to 15% of Physical Damage dealt by Supported Skill
- **Supported Skills** (183): Firebolt, Ice Nova, Leap Slam, Shield Charge, Detonate Dead, Volatile Dead, Flicker Strike, Spark, Frost Wall, Enervating Nova, Lightning Warp, Armour Breaker, Rain of #### Clash
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, Melee
- **Category**: Clash
- **Description**: Supports Melee Attack Skills. Supported Skills deal more Damage while you have a lower percentage of your Life remaining than the target struck, but less Damage when the reverse is true.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills deal 40% more Melee Damage against Enemies with a higher percentage of their Life remaining than you, but deal 20% less Melee Damage against Enemies with a lower percentage of their Life remaining than you
- **Supported Skills** (63): Leap Slam, Shield Charge, Flicker Strike, Armour Breaker, Falling Thunder, Earthquake, Sunder, Earthshatter, Boneshatter, Volcanic Fissure, Rapid Assault, Disengage, Blood Hunt, Whirling Slash, Spearfield, Whirling Assault, Rolling Slam, Supercharged Slam, Wind Blast, Wave of Frost, Ice Strike, Glacial Cascade, Killing Palm, Shattering Palm, Rampage, Furious Slam, Tempest Flurry, Staggering Palm, Siphoning Strike, Tempest Bell, Frozen Locus, Perfect Strike, Raise Shield, Resonating Shield, Thunderous Leap, Hammer of the Gods, Stampede, Shield Wall, Punch, Quarterstaff Strike, Flail Strike, Sword Slash, Axe Slash, Mace Strike, Claw Stab, Dagger Stab, Spear Stab, Vaulting Impact, Storm Wave, Gathering Storm, Primal Strikes, Cull The Weak, Fangs of Frost, Wind Serpent's Fury, Rake, Parry, Elemental Sundering, Wing Blast, Fury of the Mountain, Cross Slash, Lunar Assault, Devour, Forge Hammer

#### Splinter Totem I
- **Tags**: Support, Totem
- **Category**: Totemic Control
- **Description**: Supports Skills which create Totems, preventing having more than one active Totem but causing that Totem to splinter into smaller versions of itself after it uses an Attack or Spell, with each Totem becoming less effective. Each splintered Totem can further splinter, up to a maximum. Does not Support Skills used by Minions. Only one Totem can be splintering at a time.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills can only have one active Totem
- **Supported Skills** (4): Shockwave Totem, Siege Ballista, Artillery Ballista, Dark Effigy

### Tier 4

#### Aftershock II
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, Melee, Slam
- **Category**: Aftershock
- **Description**: Supports Slams you use yourself, giving them a chance to create an Aftershock.

#### Brambleslam
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, AoE, Melee, Slam, Trigger, Physical, Hazard, Plant
- **Category**: Brambleslam
- **Description**: Supports Slam Skills. Supported Skills create Hazardous Brambles on the ground that activate after a duration. Enemies which come in contact with these thorns take damage and are Maimed. A maximum of 20 Brambles are allowed at one time. Does not modify Skills used by Minions or Totems.
- **Mods**: Supported Slams create 3 Brambles
- **Supported Skills** (17): Leap Slam, Falling Thunder, Earthquake, Sunder, Earthshatter, Volcanic Fissure, Rolling Slam, Supercharged Slam, Rampage, Furious Slam, Thunderous Leap, Hammer of the Gods, Stampede, Vaulting Impact, Fury of the Mountain, Devour, Forge Hammer

#### Branching Fissures II
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Fissures
- **Description**: Supports Skills which create Fissures in the ground, causing them to create additional secondary Fissures which branch off from the primary fissure, with lowered area of effect and Damage.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills' Fissures branch 2 times
- **Supported Skills** (8): Sunder, Earthshatter, Volcanic Fissure, Glacial Cascade, Storm Wave, Entangle, Fury of the Mountain, Forge Hammer

- **Tags**: Support, Minion, AoE, Fire
- **Category**: Infernal Legion
- **Description**: Supports skills which create Minions which can be damaged, causing them and enemies near them to Burn. Damage dealt by the Burning is based off the Life of the supported Minion.
- **Mods**: Minions from Supported Skills take 30% of their maximum Life as Fire Damage per second

- **Category**: Refraction
- **Description**: Supports Banner Skills, causing Enemies within their area to gain Refractive Dissolution, a Debuff which lowers Elemental Resistances.

- **Tags**: Support, Totem
- **Category**: Reinforced Totems
- **Description**: Supports Skills which create Totems. Totems created by Supported Skills have additional Elemental Resistances.

#### Splinter Totem II
- **Tags**: Support, Totem
- **Category**: Totemic Control
- **Description**: Supports Skills which create Totems, preventing having more than one active Totem but causing that Totem to splinter into smaller versions of itself after it uses an Attack or Spell, with each Totem becoming less effective. Each splintered Totem can further splinter, up to a maximum. Does not Support Skills used by Minions. Only one Totem can be splintering at a time.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills can only have one active Totem
- **Supported Skills** (4): Shockwave Totem, Siege Ballista, Artillery Ballista, Dark Effigy

#### Overabundance I
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Overabundance
- **Description**: Supports skills which can have a Limited number of effects active at once, increasing that Limit at the cost of their duration. Only applies to restrictions that use the word "Limit".
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have +1 to Limit
- **Supported Skills** (46): Raise Zombie, Sniper's Mark, Firestorm, Shockwave Totem, Bone Offering, Frost Bomb, Orb of Storms, Earthquake, Siege Ballista, Earthshatter, Sigil of Power, Tornado, Galvanic Field, Volcanic Fissure, Artillery Ballista, Volcano, Thunderstorm, Gas Grenade, Pain Offering, Tempest Bell, Frozen Locus, Unearth, Toxic Growth, Gas Arrow, Solar Orb, Vine Arrow, Decompose, Raging Spirits, Explosive Spear, Profane Ritual, Soul Offering, Dark Effigy, Living Bomb, Shield Wall, Freezing Mark, Voltaic Mark, Tornado Shot, Ravenous Swarm, Whirlwind Lance, Bloodhound's Mark, Storm Lance, Entangle, Thrashing Vines, Forge Hammer, Briarpatch, Mirror of Refraction

#### Overabundance III
- **Tags**: Support, Curse
- **Category**: Overabundance
- **Description**: Supports skills which can have a Limited number of effects active at once, doubling that Limit at the cost of Cursing yourself on Skill use. Only applies to restrictions that use the word "Limit".
- **Mods**: Inflicts a random Curse on you when you use Supported Skills, ignoring Curse limit

#### Pursuit I

- **Category**: Pursuit
- **Description**: Supports Melee Attacks. Supported Skills deal more Melee damage if you have struck with a Projectile Attack Hit in the last eight seconds, but cannot themselves deal Projectile Damage.

#### Rakiata's Flow
- **Tags**: Support, Lineage
- **Category**: Rakiata's Flow
- **Requires**: Level 65

#### Tasalio's Rhythm
- **Tags**: Support, Lineage
- **Category**: Perfection
- **Requires**: Level 65
- **Description**: Supports Skills which have a benefit for Perfectly Timing their use. On successfully executing Perfect Timing with Supported Skills, gain Tasalio's Rhythm. Tasalio's Rhythm causes Supported Skills to deal more damage and have shorter Perfect Timing windows for each stack. Failing to execute any Perfect Timing (even with skills not supported by Tasalio's Rhythm) will remove all Tasalio's Rhythm on you.
- **Mods**: Successfully executing Perfect Timing with Supported Skills grants a stack of Tasalio's Rhythm / All Tasalio's Rhythm is lost on failing to execute any Perfect Timing /  Supported Skills deal 10% more Damage for each stack of Tasalio's Rhythm /  Supported Skills have a 30% shorter Perfect Timing window for each stack of Tasalio's Rhythm /  Tasalio's Rhythm stacks up to 5 times
- **Supported Skills** (3): Snipe, Perfect Strike, Gathering Storm

#### Window of Opportunity I
- **Tags**: Support, Channelling
- **Category**: Window of Opportunity
- **Description**: Supports Channelling skills that have special effects if released with Perfect Timing, causing them to deal much more damage if released with Perfect Timing but reducing the Perfect Timing window.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have a 35% shorter Perfect Timing window
- **Supported Skills** (3): Snipe, Perfect Strike, Gathering Storm

### Tier 2

#### Adhesive Grenades I
- **Tags**: Support, Grenade
- **Category**: Adhesive Grenades
- **Description**: Supports Grenade Skills. Grenades from Supported Skills do not bounce, instead halting movement where they intially land, but doing lower damage when they detonate.
- **Mods**: Supported Grenade Skills stop where they initially land
- **Supported Skills** (6): Explosive Grenade, Flash Grenade, Gas Grenade, Oil Grenade, Voltaic Grenade, Cluster Grenade

#### Cadence
- **Tags**: Support, Attack
- **Category**: Cadence
- **Description**: Supports Attacks you use yourself. Supported Skills gain more Attack speed each time you use them, but will become unusable if used too frequently in a short time frame. Sustained Skills will instead gain Attack speed periodically while being used.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have 8% more Attack speed for each time they've been used Recently

#### Commiserate
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Commiserate
- **Description**: Supports Skills you use yourself or Trigger, which can cause Damaging Hits. Supported Skills inflict more powerful Ailments if you are afflicted with those Ailments when you inflict them, while also removing from you any Ailment that they inflict.

#### Delayed Gratification
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Delayed Gratification
- **Description**: Supports Skills which require some Condition to be met for use. Supported Skills can be used an additional time after their Condition has been met, but meeting that Condition is harder.
- **Mods**: Supported Conditional Skills can be used an additional time within 10 seconds of using them after meeting their requirements
- **Supported Skills** (10): Charged Staff, Tempest Bell, Hammer of the Gods, Mantra of Destruction, Unbound Avatar, Wind Serpent's Fury, Spear of Solaris, Ancestral Cry, Walking Calamity, Apocalypse

#### Durability
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Durability
- **Description**: Supports Skills which create objects that are destroyed after being Hit a number of times, allowing for them to last for additional Hits. Does not modify Skills used by Minions.
- **Mods**: Objects created by Supported Skills can be Hit +2 times
- **Supported Skills** (4): Tempest Bell, Lightning Rod, Shockchain Arrow, Tornado Shot

#### Electrocute
- **Tags**: Support, Lightning
- **Category**: Electrocute
- **Description**: Supports any Skill which can deal Damage. Lightning Damage from Supported Skills can inflict Electrocute, but Supported Skills cannot inflict Shock.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills Cannot inflict Shock

#### Overreach
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, AoE
- **Category**: Increased Area of Effect
- **Description**: Supports Attack Skills which deal Damage in an Area. Supported Skills have significantly increased Area of Effect, but are less Accurate against nearby targets.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have 40% increased Area of Effect

- **Tags**: Support, AoE, Duration
- **Category**: Shocking Leap
- **Description**: Supports Skills that leap into the air and deal damage, causing them to create Shocked Ground the first time they Critically Hit an enemy.

#### Volt

- **Category**: Volt
- **Description**: Supports Projectile Attack Skills you use yourself. Supported Skills gain Voltaic Charge as you move, up to a maximum. When used, Supported Skills expend that Charge to gain extra Lightning Damage.

### Tier 3

#### Adhesive Grenades II
- **Tags**: Support, Grenade
- **Category**: Adhesive Grenades
- **Description**: Supports Grenade Skills. Grenades from Supported Skills do not bounce, instead halting movement where they intially land.
- **Mods**: Supported Grenade Skills stop where they initially land
- **Supported Skills** (6): Explosive Grenade, Flash Grenade, Gas Grenade, Oil Grenade, Voltaic Grenade, Cluster Grenade

#### Alignment I
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, Projectile
- **Category**: Alignment
- **Description**: Supports Bow Attacks. Supported Skills indicate one of four directions, changing indicated direction when an Attack with Supported Skill matches that direction. Attacks from Supported Skills which match the indicated direction deal much more Damage. Cannot Support Channelled Skills.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills indicate one of four directions / Indicated direction changes when an Attack with Supported Skill matches indicated direction
- **Supported Skills** (17): Rain of Arrows, Lightning Arrow, Escape Shot, Spiral Volley, Poisonburst Arrow, Toxic Growth, Stormcaller Arrow, Lightning Rod, Gas Arrow, Electrocuting Arrow, Vine Arrow, Bow Shot, Shockchain Arrow, Ice Shot, Tornado Shot, Magnetic Salvo, Freezing Salvo

#### Caltrops

#### Neural Overload
- **Tags**: Support, Lightning
- **Category**: Electrocute
- **Description**: Supports any skill that Hits enemies. Nearby enemies are marked when they are Primed for Electrocution, and hitting a marked enemy with a supported skill will Electrocute them.

#### Cooldown Recovery II
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Cooldown Recovery

#### Delayed Reaction

- **Category**: Delayed Reaction

#### Hit and Run

#### Perfected Endurance
- **Tags**: Support, Channelling
- **Category**: Perfected Endurance
- **Description**: Supports skills which have a benefit for Perfect Timing. Supported Skills grant at least one Endurance Charge when Hitting an enemy with Perfect Timing.
- **Mods**: Gain an Endurance Charge when hitting an Enemy with Supported Skill when Perfectly Timed
- **Supported Skills** (3): Snipe, Perfect Strike, Gathering Storm

#### Perfection
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Perfection
- **Description**: Supports skills which have a benefit for Perfectly Timing their use. On successfully executing Perfect Timing with Supported Skills, gain Perfection, which is a powerful damage buff. However, failing to execute any Perfect Timing (even with skills not supported by Perfection) will remove all Perfection on you.
- **Mods**: Successfully executing Perfect Timing with Supported Skills grants Perfection / All Perfection is lost on failing to execute any Perfect Timing
- **Supported Skills** (3): Snipe, Perfect Strike, Gathering Storm

#### Spectral Volley
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, Projectile
- **Category**: Spectral Volley
- **Description**: Supports Bow or Spear Projectile Attacks you use yourself. Supported Skills deal lower damage initially, but generate Spectral Projectiles, which deal more damage when they fire. Spectral Projectiles linger and will fire a short duration after no new Spectral Projectiles have been created. Cannot support Channelling Skills, Leaping skills, or skills which rain Projectiles from above.
- **Mods**: Attacks with Supported Skills create a Spectral Projectile
- **Supported Skills** (18): Lightning Arrow, Lightning Spear, Glacial Lance, Spiral Volley, Poisonburst Arrow, Stormcaller Arrow, Gas Arrow, Electrocuting Arrow, Twister, Explosive Spear, Spear Throw, Bow Shot, Shockchain Arrow, Ice Shot, Magnetic Salvo, Freezing Salvo, Whirlwind Lance, Storm Lance

### Tier 5

#### Alignment III
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, Projectile
- **Category**: Alignment, Additional Projectiles
- **Description**: Supports Bow Attacks. Supported Skills indicate one of four directions, changing indicated direction when an Attack with Supported Skill matches that direction. Attacks from Supported Skills which match the indicated direction fire additional Projectiles. Cannot Support Channelled Skills.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills indicate one of four directions / Indicated direction changes when an Attack with Supported Skill matches indicated direction
- **Supported Skills** (17): Rain of Arrows, Lightning Arrow, Escape Shot, Spiral Volley, Poisonburst Arrow, Toxic Growth, Stormcaller Arrow, Lightning Rod, Gas Arrow, Electrocuting Arrow, Vine Arrow, Bow Shot, Shockchain Arrow, Ice Shot, Tornado Shot, Magnetic Salvo, Freezing Salvo

#### Ammo Conservation III
- **Tags**: Support, Ammunition, Projectile
- **Category**: Ammo Conservation
- **Description**: Supports Crossbow Ammunition Skills, granting a chance to not consume a Bolt when firing, at the cost of Reload speed.
- **Mods**: Bolts fired by Supported Crossbow Attacks have 30% chance to not expend Ammunition

#### Second Wind III
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Second Wind
- **Description**: Supports Skills which have a cooldown, giving them extra uses of that cooldown and causing them to recover your Life when a Skill is used and goes on cooldown. Cannot support Meta, instant, or Triggered Skills, and cannot modify the Skills of Minions.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have 40% less Cooldown Recovery Rate

#### Swift Affliction III
- **Tags**: Support, Duration
- **Category**: Swift Affliction

- **Description**: Supports Spells you cast yourself, making their effect reoccur up to five times when cast, but giving them a moderate Cooldown. Cannot support Channelling Skills.
- **Mods**: Supported Spells gain a Seal every 50% of cast time, to a maximum of 5 Seals / Supported Spells are Unsealed when cast, and their effects Reoccur for each Seal lost
- **Supported Skills** (44): Firebolt, Ice Nova, Detonate Dead, Volatile Dead, Spark, Enervating Nova, Temporal Chains, Enfeeble, Despair, Lightning Warp, Firestorm, Arc, Flammability, Hypothermia, Conductivity, Elemental Weakness, Ball Lightning, Orb of Storms, Contagion, Essence Drain, Frostbolt, Dark Pact, Vulnerability, Soulrend, Flame Wall, Hexblast, Exsanguinate, Comet, [DNT] Crushing Earth, Lightning Bolt, Chaos Bolt, Bone Cage, Unearth, Solar Orb, Fireball, Snap, Freezing Shards, Profane Ritual, Bone Blast, Ember Fusillade, Inevitable Agony, Entangle, Feast of Flesh, Frost Darts

#### Zenith I
- **Tags**: Support, Spell
- **Category**: Zenith
- **Description**: Supports Spell Skills. Supported Skills deal more damage while you are above 90% of your Maximum Mana. Does not modify Skills used by Minions.
- **Mods**: Supported Spells deal 30% more Damage while you are above 90% of your Maximum Mana
- **Supported Skills** (55): Firebolt, Ice Nova, Detonate Dead, Volatile Dead, Spark, Frost Wall, Enervating Nova, Lightning Warp, Firestorm, Power Siphon, Arc, Arctic Armour, Incinerate, Flameblast, Ball Lightning, Frost Bomb, Orb of Storms, Contagion, Essence Drain, Frostbolt, Dark Pact, Soulrend, Flame Wall, Hexblast, Exsanguinate, Reap, Eye of Winter, Tornado, Lightning Conduit, Galvanic Field, Comet, [DNT] Crushing Earth, Volcano, Lightning Bolt, Thunderstorm, Chaos Bolt, Bonestorm, Bone Cage, Unearth, Solar Orb, Fireball, Snap, Freezing Shards, Decompose, Profane Ritual, Bone Blast, Living Bomb, Ember Fusillade, Elemental Storm, Elemental Expression, Moment of Vulnerability, Entangle, Thrashing Vines, Frost Darts, Apocalypse

### Tier 2

#### Abiding Hex
- **Tags**: Support, Curse
- **Category**: Abiding Hex
- **Description**: Supports Curse Skills you cast yourself. Supported Skills will consume Power Charges on use, gaining significant Curse duration if they do.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills consume a Power Charge on use / Supported Skills have 80% more duration when consuming a Power Charge
- **Supported Skills** (9): Temporal Chains, Enfeeble, Despair, Flammability, Hypothermia, Conductivity, Elemental Weakness, Vulnerability, Inevitable Agony

#### Accelerated Growth
- **Tags**: Support, Spell, AoE, Trigger, Plant
- **Category**: Accelerated Growth
- **Description**: Supports Plant Skills, causing them to Trigger an explosion after they have been Overgrown.
- **Mods**: Triggers Accelerated Growth on Overgrowing Plants created by Supported Skills
- **Supported Skills** (6): Toxic Growth, Vine Arrow, Entangle, Thrashing Vines, Toxic Domain, Briarpatch

#### Acrimony
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Acrimony
- **Description**: Supports Skills which can Damage Enemies. Enemies affected by Damage over time from Supported Skills which was not caused by a Damaging Ailment have reduced Life regeneration rate. Only the strongest instance of this Debuff will apply. Does not Support Skills used by Minions.
- **Mods**: Enemies affected by non-Ailment Damage over time from Supported Skills have 50% reduced Life regeneration rate
- **Supported Skills** (12): Incinerate, Herald of Ash, Contagion, Essence Drain, Soulrend, Flame Wall, Exsanguinate, Tornado, Vine Arrow, Profane Ritual, Tornado Shot, Blood Boil

#### Danse Macabre
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Danse Macabre
- **Description**: Supports Offering Skills. Supported Skills have increased Buff effect and deal more damage, but will target an additional skeletal Minion when cast. If there is not an additional skeletal Minion to target, no damage or Buff effect will be granted.
- **Mods**: Supported Offering Skills have 30% increased Buff effect

#### Font of Mana
- **Tags**: Support, Totem
- **Category**: Font
- **Description**: Supports Skills which create Totems. Totems created by supported Skills generate a Font of Mana which will Leech Mana to Allies within it.

#### Spell Echo
- **Tags**: Support, Spell, AoE
- **Category**: Spell Echo
- **Description**: Supports Spells that affect an area around you or a target location. Supported Spells echo, causing their effects to happen again after a short delay. Cannot support Channelling skills Remote skills or skills which are Triggered.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have 30% less Cast Speed
- **Supported Skills** (28): Ice Nova, Detonate Dead, Volatile Dead, Frost Wall, Enervating Nova, Temporal Chains, Enfeeble, Despair, Firestorm, Flammability, Hypothermia, Conductivity, Elemental Weakness, Frost Bomb, Vulnerability, Flame Wall, Hexblast, Comet, [DNT] Crushing Earth, Consecrate, Lightning Bolt, Thunderstorm, Bone Cage, Snap, Profane Ritual, Bone Blast, Inevitable Agony, Thrashing Vines

#### Upwelling I
- **Tags**: Support, Buff, Persistent
- **Category**: Upwellling
- **Description**: Supports Persistent Buff Skills, causing your Minions to deal increased Damage while you are not on full Mana while the Supported Skill is active.
- **Mods**: Your Minions deal 30% increased Damage while you are not on full Mana while a Supported Skill is active
- **Supported Skills** (58): Discipline, Arctic Armour, Purity of Fire, Purity of Ice, Purity of Lightning, Impurity, Herald of Ash, Herald of Ice, Herald of Thunder, Plague Bearer, Lingering Illusion, Ghost Dance, Mana Remnants, Magma Barrier, Rhoa Mount, Raging Spirits, Wind Dancer, Grim Feast, Scavenged Plating, Blink, Malice, Life Remnants, War Banner, Defiance Banner, Dread Banner, Align Fate, Temporal Rift, Sorcery Ward, Time of Need, Attrition, Elemental Conflux, Into the Breach, Charge Regulation, Shard Scavenger, Overwhelming Presence, Alchemist's Boon, Sacrifice, Archmage, Berserk, Herald of Plague, Herald of Blood, Withering Presence, Ravenous Swarm, Combat Frenzy, Blood Boil, Trinity, Trail of Caltrops, Convalescence, Void Illusion, Iron Ward, Heart of Ice, Fulmination, Siphon Elements, Briarpatch, Eternal Rage, Savage Fury, Mirror of Refraction, Barkskin

#### Chaotic Freeze
- **Tags**: Support, Spell, Chaos
- **Category**: Chaotic Freeze
- **Description**: Supports Spells that deal non-Ailment Chaos damage over time. Enemies taking damage over time from Debuffs caused by supported skills will suffer Freeze build up from Chaos damage Hits from any source. Does not Support Skills used by Minions.
- **Mods**: Chaos damage Contributes to Freeze buildup for Hits against targets taking damage over time from Supported Skills
- **Supported Skills** (4): Contagion, Essence Drain, Soulrend, Profane Ritual

#### Corpse Conservation
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Corpse Conservation
- **Description**: Supports skills that consume Corpses, giving them a chance to take effect without destroying the Corpse.
- **Mods**: Corpses consumed by Supported Skills have 25% chance to not be destroyed
- **Supported Skills** (10): Detonate Dead, Volatile Dead, Raise Zombie, Unearth, Decompose, Profane Ritual, Kelari's Malediction, Ritual Sacrifice, Devour, Feast of Flesh

#### Cursed Ground
- **Tags**: Support, Curse
- **Category**: Cursed Ground
- **Description**: Supports Curse Skills. Supported Curse Skills create areas which Curse Enemies so long as they are within them.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills create Cursed Ground / Enemies on the Cursed Ground from a Supported Skill are Cursed while within it
- **Supported Skills** (9): Temporal Chains, Enfeeble, Despair, Flammability, Hypothermia, Conductivity, Elemental Weakness, Vulnerability, Inevitable Agony

#### Decaying Hex
- **Tags**: Support, Chaos, Curse
- **Category**: Decaying Hex
- **Description**: Supports Curse skills. Cursed enemies' bodies decay, taking Chaos damage over time.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills inflict Decay, dealing 100% of Intelligence as Chaos damage per second for 8 seconds
- **Supported Skills** (9): Temporal Chains, Enfeeble, Despair, Flammability, Hypothermia, Conductivity, Elemental Weakness, Vulnerability, Inevitable Agony

#### Drain Ailments
- **Tags**: Support, Spell
- **Category**: Drain Ailments
- **Description**: Supports Spells that deal non-Ailment damage over time, causing them to consume Ailments on enemies it applies damage over time Debuffs to in order to deal substantially more damage over time.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills Consume all Ailments of a random type on the target when inflicting damage over time Debuffs, causing the Debuff to deal 35% more damage if any Ailments were consumed
- **Supported Skills** (8): Incinerate, Contagion, Essence Drain, Soulrend, Flame Wall, Exsanguinate, Tornado, Profane Ritual

#### Electromagnetism
- **Tags**: Support, Spell, AoE, Trigger, Sustained, Lightning, Payoff
- **Category**: Electromagnetism
- **Description**: Supports Skills that Hit enemies. When Supported Skills Shock an enemy that is nearby other Shocked enemies, trigger Electromagnetism, sucking in nearby enemies, Hindering them, and dealing Lightning damage at an interval.
- **Mods**: On Shocking an enemy where there are at least 3 / Shocked enemies within 4 metres that are not already / in a Shocking Rift, Supported Skills Consume Shock of / all enemies within 4 metres to trigger Shocking Rift

#### Energy Capacitor
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Energy Capacitor
- **Description**: Supports Invocation Skills which Trigger other Skills. Supported Skills have significantly higher Maximum Energy.
- **Mods**: Supported Meta Gems have 80% increased Maximum Energy

#### Energy Retention
- **Tags**: Support, Trigger
- **Category**: Energy Retention
- **Description**: Supports Meta Skills. Supported Skills gain a chance to partially Refund a portion of Energy cost when Triggering or Invoking other Skills.
- **Mods**: Skills Triggered by Supported Meta Skills / have 35% chance to refund half of their Energy cost
- **Supported Skills** (1): Trail of Caltrops

#### Essence Harvest
- **Tags**: Support, Minion, Persistent
- **Category**: Essence Harvest
- **Description**: Supports Skills which create Reviving Persistent Minions. When those Minions die, you Recoup a percentage of your maximum Mana.
- **Mods**: Recoup 8% of your maximum Mana when a Persistent Reviving Minion created by Supported Skill dies
- **Supported Skills** (11): Skeletal Warrior, Skeletal Reaver, Skeletal Brute, Skeletal Sniper, Skeletal Frost Mage, Skeletal Storm Mage, Skeletal Arsonist, Skeletal Cleric, Wolf Pack, Summon Infernal Hound, Companion: {0}

#### Eternal Mark
- **Tags**: Support, Mark
- **Category**: Eternal Mark
- **Description**: Supports Mark Skills, causing them to not be Consumed the first time they are Activated.
- **Mods**: Marks from Supported Skills are not Consumed the / first time they Activate
- **Supported Skills** (4): Sniper's Mark, Freezing Mark, Voltaic Mark, Bloodhound's Mark

#### Fluke
- **Tags**: Support, Trigger
- **Category**: Fluke
- **Description**: Supports Skills which Trigger other Skills. Skills Triggered by Supported Skills have their Damage randomly raised or lowered when Triggered, as well as recovering a random amount of their cost when Triggered.
- **Mods**: Skills Triggered by Supported Skills deal between 40% less and 60% more Damage
- **Supported Skills** (3): Trail of Caltrops, Ancestral Cry, Apocalypse

#### Fortress II
- **Tags**: Support
- **Category**: Fortress
- **Description**: Supports skills that create walls in a line, causing them to be created in a circle instead but deal less Hit damage and have lowered Area of Effect.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have 20% less Area of Effect
- **Supported Skills** (3): Frost Wall, Flame Wall, Shield Wall

- **Category**: Burgeon

- **Category**: Clarity

#### Catalysing Elements
- **Tags**: Support, Spell, AoE, Trigger, Lightning, Cold, Fire
- **Category**: Elemental Discharge
- **Description**: Supports Skills which are boosted by Elemental Ground Surfaces, Triggering Catalysing Discharge of the corresponding type when they are boosted by an allied Elemental Ground Surface.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills Trigger Catalysing Discharge when boosted by an Elemental Ground Surface
- **Supported Skills** (5): Eye of Winter, Tornado, Whirling Slash, Twister, Whirlwind Lance

#### Chaos Mastery
- **Tags**: Support, Chaos
- **Category**: Mastery
- **Description**: Supports Chaos skills, granting them an additional level. Does not support skills which do not have levels.
- **Mods**: +1 to Level of Supported Chaos Skills
- **Supported Skills** (23): Despair, Impurity, Contagion, Wither, Essence Drain, Dark Pact, Skeletal Sniper, Soulrend, Hexblast, Gas Grenade, Chaos Bolt, Poisonburst Arrow, Toxic Growth, Gas Arrow, Vine Arrow, Decompose, Profane Ritual, Dark Effigy, Mantra of Destruction, Herald of Plague, Withering Presence, Ravenous Swarm, Toxic Domain

#### Crescendo III
- **Tags**: Support, Attack, Melee, Strike
- **Category**: Crescendo
- **Description**: Supports Strikes that perform a Final Strike at the end of a combination of attacks, causing the Final Strike to be Ancestrally Boosted.
- **Mods**: Final Strike of Supported Skill is Ancestrally Boosted
- **Supported Skills** (3): Ice Strike, Tempest Flurry, Primal Strikes

#### Expand
- **Tags**: Support, Spell, AoE
- **Category**: Seal, Increased Area of Effect
- **Description**: Supports Spells you cast yourself, increasing their area of effect when cast. Cannot support Channelling Skills or Skills with a Cooldown.
- **Mods**: Supported Spells gain a Seal every 200% of cast time, to a maximum of 3 Seals / Supported Spells are Unsealed when cast, and their area of effect is increased for each Seal lost
- **Supported Skills** (45): Firebolt, Ice Nova, Detonate Dead, Volatile Dead, Enervating Nova, Temporal Chains, Enfeeble, Despair, Lightning Warp, Firestorm, Flammability, Hypothermia, Conductivity, Elemental Weakness, Ball Lightning, Orb of Storms, Contagion, Frostbolt, Dark Pact, Vulnerability, Flame Wall, Hexblast, Reap, Tornado, Galvanic Field, Comet, [DNT] Crushing Earth, Consecrate, Lightning Bolt, Thunderstorm, Bone Cage, Unearth, Solar Orb, Fireball, Decompose, Profane Ritual, Bone Blast, Living Bomb, Ember Fusillade, Inevitable Agony, Entangle, Thrashing Vines, Feast of Flesh, Frost Darts, Apocalypse

#### Profanity II
- **Tags**: Support, Chaos
- **Category**: Profanity
- **Description**: Supports Skills you use yourself. Supported Skills consume many Corpses on use, dealing more Chaos Damage per Corpse consumed. Cannot support Triggered Skills or Reservation Skills.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills consume up to 10 Corpses within 5 metres / on use, if possible

#### Rapid Casting III
- **Tags**: Support, Spell
- **Category**: Rapid Casting
- **Description**: Supports Spells, causing them to cast faster for each different Spell you've cast Recently.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have 10% increased Cast Speed for each different Spell you've Cast in the last eight seconds
- **Supported Skills** (82): Firebolt, Ice Nova, Detonate Dead, Volatile Dead, Spark, Frost Wall, Enervating Nova, Temporal Chains, Enfeeble, Despair, Lightning Warp, Firestorm, Power Siphon, Arc, Arctic Armour, Flammability, Hypothermia, Conductivity, Elemental Weakness, Incinerate, Flameblast, Barrage, Ball Lightning, Frost Bomb, Orb of Storms, Contagion, Wither, Essence Drain, Frostbolt, Dark Pact, Vulnerability, Soulrend, Sigil of Power, Flame Wall, Hexblast, Exsanguinate, Reap, Eye of Winter, Tornado, Lightning Conduit, Galvanic Field, Comet, [DNT] Crushing Earth, Consecrate, Mana Tempest, Volcano, Lightning Bolt, Unleash, Thunderstorm, Charged Staff, Chaos Bolt, Bonestorm, Bone Cage, Unearth, Solar Orb, Fireball, Snap, Freezing Shards, Decompose, Profane Ritual, Mana Drain, Bone Blast, Living Bomb, Ember Fusillade, Meditate, Elemental Storm, Elemental Expression, Encase in Jade, Moment of Vulnerability, Time Freeze, Time Snap, Sorcery Ward, Blink, Inevitable Agony, Entangle, Heart of Ice, Thrashing Vines, Feast of Flesh, Ice-Tipped Arrows, Frost Darts, Briarpatch, Apocalypse

#### Wildshards II
- **Tags**: Support, Spell, Projectile
- **Category**: Additional Projectiles
- **Description**: Supports Projectile Spells. Supported Spells have a chance to fire many additional Projectiles in a circle.
- **Mods**: Supported Skills have a 25% chance to fire 8 additional Projectiles in a circle
- **Supported Skills** (16): Firebolt, Spark, Arc, Ball Lightning, Essence Drain, Frostbolt, Soulrend, Eye of Winter, Volcano, Chaos Bolt, Bonestorm, Fireball, Freezing Shards, Ember Fusillade, Elemental Expression, Frost Darts
